 How to worship on Krishna Janmashtami - Eat light meals on the night before the fast and observe Brahmacharya
 - surya, som, yama, kaal, sandhi, bhoot, pawan, dikpati, bhoomi, akaash, khechar, amar or brahmadi ko namaskara kar purv yaa uttar mukh baithen
 - On the day of fast, retire from bathing routine
 - iske baad jal, fal, kush or gandh lekar sankalp karen:mamakhilpapaprashamanpurvak sarvabhisht siddhye shrikrishna janmashtami vratamahan karishye
- ab shaam ke samay kaale tilon ke jal se snaan kar devkiji ke liye 'sutikagrih' niyat karen
 - After this install the idol or picture of Lord Krishna
 - murti main balak shrikrishna ko stanpan karaati hui devaki hon or lakshmi unke charan sparsh kiye hon agar aisa chitra mil jaae to behatar rahata he
 - After this, worship the law

 Charles de Gaul, then President of France, said that France could not arrest its Voltaire
 lekin jetali apane lekhakon kii baat sunne kii jagah, unki asahmati kaa sammaan karne yaa usko sahan bhar karne kii jagah unhen baagi qaraar dete hai, un par saazish kaa ilzaam lagaate hai, unhen pryojit virodh kaa mujrim tehra dete hai

 magar yah khel kab tak chupa rahegaa, yah dekhne kii baat he

 ) maharashtra kii ratnagiri-sindhudurg loksabhaa seat par tisare charan main yani 23 april ko vot daale jaaenge
 There are 12 candidates in the fray for the 2019 Lok Sabha elections in ratnagiri-sindhudurg seat of Maharashtra
 shivasena ne apane maujuuda saansad vinayak raut ko tikat diya he to vahiin congress se naveenchandra bhalchandra bandivdekar ko apana ummidavaar banaaya he
 Kishore Siddu Vark from Bahujan Samaj Party (BSP), Nilesh Narayan Rane from Maharashtra Swabhiman Paksha and Bhikuram Kashiram Palkar from Bahujan Mukti Party are contesting
 vanchit bahujan aghadi se maaruti ramchandra joshi or bahujan republican socialist party se rajesh dilipakumaar jadhav chunaav maidan main hai
 Apart from this, four independent candidates have also gone to the polls
 maharashtra kii kul 48 loksabhaa siton par 4 charnon main matdaan hoga, jisamen ratnagiri-sindhudurg seat par tisare charan main vot daale jaaenge
